 ' The Vedic period is a period segment of ancient Indian culture
 us dauraan vedon kii rachana hui thi
 After the fall of Harappan culture, a new civilization emerged in India
 is sabhyataa kii jaankaree ke strot vedon ke aadhaar par ise vaidic sabhyataa kaa naam diya gaya
 (1) Vedic period split into two parts Rigvedic period - 1500-1000 AD
 pus
 And the later Vedic period - 1000‚Äì600 AD
 pus
 Has been done in (2)arya sarvapratham punjab or afghanistan main based the
 Max M√ºller considered Central Asia to be the abode of the Aryans
 aaryon dwaara nirmit sabhyataa hi vaidic sabhyataa kahalaai he
 (3) The civilization developed by the Aryans was rural civilization
 rigvedikkaleen devtadevatasambandhindrayuddh kaa netaa or varsha kaa devatoagnidevtaa or manushya ke bich madhyasthvarunaprithvi or surya ke nirmaataa,samudr kaa devtaa,vishwa ke niamak evam shaasha,satya kaa pratik,ritu parivartan evam din-raat kaa kartadyoakash kaa devtaa(sabase pracheen)somvanaspati devataushapragati evam utthan devataasvinavipattiyon ko haranevaale devatapushanapashuon kaa devatavishnuvishwa ke sangrakshak or paalankartamrutandhi-tufaan kaa devtaa(4)aaryon kii bhashaa sanskrit thi
 (5) The administrative unit of the Aryans was divided into five parts: (i) Total (ii) Village (iii) Vish (iv) Jan (iv) Nation
 (6)vaidic kaal main rajtantratmak pranali prachlit thi
 (7) The head of the village was called Gramini and the head of Vish was called Vishpati
 jan ke shaasha ko rajan kaha jaataa tha
 Purohit and fighter were the chief among the officials
 (8)shashan kaa pramukh raja hota tha
 The king was hereditary but the public could remove him
 vah kshetra vishesh kaa nahin balki jan vishesh kaa pradhan hota tha
 (9) The king was the leader of the war
 use kar vasuulne kaa adhikaar nahin tha
 The king used to spend the money with whatever he wanted
 (10)raja kaa prashasnic sahyog purohit or senaanee 12 ratnin karte the
 The head of the pasture was called Vajrapati and the head of the fighting parties was called Gramini
 (11)12 ratnin is prakaar the: purohit- raja kaa pramukh paramarshdaata, senaanee- sena kaa pramukh, gramin- gram kaa sainik padaadhikari, mahishi- raja kii patni, soot- raja kaa sarathi, kshatri- pratihaar, sangrahit- koshadhyaksh, bhagadudh- kar ekatra karne vaala adhikari, akshavap- lekhadhikari, govikrut- van kaa adhikari, palagal- raja kaa mitra
 (12) Purupa, Durgapati and Sparsh were the detectives who watched the movements of the people
 (13)vajpati-gochar bhoomi kaa adhikari hota tha
 (14) Used to apprehend fiery criminals
 (15)sabha or samiti raja ko salaah dene vaali sanstha thi
 (16) The Sabha was an institution of superior and elitist people, while the committee represented the general public and Vidath was the oldest institution
 rugveda main sabase zyada vidath kaa 122 baar zikr hua he
 (17) Both women and men were involved in Vidith
 navavadhuon kaa swaagat, dharmik anushthan jaise saamaajik kaary vidath main hote the
 (18) In the Atharvaveda, the assembly and the committee have been called the two daughters of Prajapati
 samiti kaa mahatvapurn kaary raja kaa chunaav karnaa tha
 The head of the committee was called Ishaan or husband
 (19)alag-alag kshetron ke alag-alag visheshgy the
 Hotri - the reciter of the Rig Veda, Udgatri - the reciter of the recitations of the Samaveda, the Adhvaryu - the reciter of the Yajurveda and the Rivindha - the caretaker of the entire Yajna
 (20)yuddh main kabeeley kaa netritv raja karata tha, yuddh ke gavishtha shabd kaa istemaal kiya jaataa tha jiskaa arth hota he gaayon kii khoj
 (21) The Dasaragana war is mentioned in the seventh mandala of the Rigveda, this battle was fought between Sudas and the ten people on the banks of river Ravi
 jisamen sudas jite the
 (22) The Rigvedic society was divided into Brahmins, Kshatriyas, Vaishyas and Shudras
 yah vibhaajan vyavsaay par aadhaarit tha
 The 10th mandala of the Rigveda states that Brahmins originated from the face of Param Purush, Kshatriyas from their arms, Vaishya from their thighs and Shudra from their feet
 pramukh darshan evam uske pravartakadarshanapravartakacharvakcharvakyogpathanjalisankhyakapilnyayagautamapurvamimasajaiminiuttaramimasabadarinvaisheshikakana yaa ulum(23)ek or varg ' paniyon ' kaa tha jo dhani the or vyapaar karte the
 (24) Beggars and agricultural slaves did not exist
 sampatti kii ikai gaay thi jo vinimay kaa madhyam bhi thi
 The charioteer and carpenter community received special honors
 (25)aaryon kaa samaaj pitrupradhan tha
 The smallest unit of the society was the family headed by a father called Kulap
 (26)mahilaayein is kaal main apane pati ke saath yajna kaary main bhaag leti thim
 (27) Child marriage and pradapratha were not prevalent during this period
 (28)vidhwaa apane pati ke chote bhai se vivaah kar sakati thi
 Widow marriage, Upanayana ritual of women, Neog Gandharva and inter-caste marriage were prevalent
 (29)mahilaayein padhai kar sakati thim
 The Rigveda describes female women like Ghosha, Apala, Vishwas
 (30)jivan bhar avivaahit rahane vaali mahila ko amaju kaha jaataa tha
 (31) The main drink of the Aryans was Somaras
 jo vanaspati se banaaya jaataa tha
 (32) Aryans used to use three types of clothes
 (i) vaas (ii) adhivaas (iii) ushshneey (iv) andar pahanane vaale kapadon ko nivi kaha jaataa tha
 Music, Rathdor, horse racing were the means of entertainment of the Aryans
 (33)aaryon kaa mukhya vyavsaay kheti or pashupaalan tha
 (34) Cows were categorized as animals not killed
 (35)gaay kii hatya karne vaale yaa use ghayal karne vaale ke khilaaf mrityudand yaa desh nikaala kii sajaa thi
 Rig Vedic Rivers Ancient Name Modern namekrubhakurramakubhabakulvasthajelamaskinchinavaparushniravishtudrisalajavipashavayasadaniragandkadushadhigghargomgalgomtisuvastusvat (36) Arya was the beloved animal of the Aryans and the beloved deity Indra
 (37)aaryon dwaara khoji gai dhaatu loha thi
 (38) The man who traveled far and wide was called Pani
 (39)len-dein main vastu-vinimay pranali maujuud thi
 (40) The person who gave interest by giving loan was called usurper
 (41)sabhi nadiyon main saraswati sabase mahatvapurn or pavitra nadi maani jaati thi
 (42) Prajapati became the beloved deity in the later Vedic period
 (43)uttaravaidic kaal main varna vyavsaay kii bajaay janm ke aadhaar par nirdhaarit hote the
 (44) In the later Vedic period the plow was called Sira and the plow line was called Sita
 (45)uttaravaidic kaal main nishk or shatmaan mudra kii ikaiyaan thim
 (46) Sankhya philosophy was the oldest of all philosophies in India
 iske anusaar mul tatv 25 hai, jinamein pehla tatv prakruti he
 (47) Satyameva Jayate is derived from Mundakopanishad
 (48)gayatri mantra savita naamak devtaa ko sambodhit he jiskaa sambandh rugveda se he
 (49) In the later Vedic period Kaushambi city used pucca bricks for the first time
 (50)mahakavy do hai- mahabharat or ramayana
 (51) The old name of Mahabharata is Jayasahita, it is the world's largest epic
 (52)sarvapratham 'jaabalopanishad ' main chaaron ashram bramhchary, grihasth, vanprastha tathaa sanyas ashram kaa ullekh miltaa he
 (53) The institution named Gotra was born in the later Vedic period
 (54)rugveda main dhaatuon main sabase pehle tambe yaa kaanse kaa zikr kiya gaya he
 They were also familiar with gold and silver
 lekin rugveda main lohe kaa zikr nahin he

 bachche khilne ke dauraan sabakuch bhul jate hai
 They do not feel heat nor fatigue while playing but the heat and heat of the sun can prove dangerous for them
 garmi lagane se ek ore jahaan kamajori ho jaati he vahiin duusari ore kai bimariyon ke hone kaa khatra bhi bad jaataa he
 Now if there are children, we cannot stop them from playing and playing, but if you want, you can keep your children safe by adopting these measures
 aaie jaane, kaise bachaaya jaae bacchon ko garmi ke kahar se
 
 
 -the digestive power of children becomes weak during the summer season
 is dauraan bacchon ko diaria, lu lagane, pet main jalan hone, ulti hone, pilia hone, typhoid hone kii ashanka bad jaati he
 So take full care of children's food and give them a light, nutritious diet
 karen
 -while playing, children forget everything and keep playing without paying attention to the weather
 aise main dhyaan rakhen ki baccha tej dhoop yaa lu ke samay na khele
 Allow the child to go out only in the evening
 din main use indor game khilne ke liye kahen
 - In summer, mosquitoes and insects become very active in the evening
 aise main jab baccha khilne ja rahaa ho to use keedon or machharon se suraksha pradaan karne vaali kriim lagaakar hi baahar bhejein
 - Try not to let the child eat anything outside
 di-hydration se bachaane ke liye bacchon ko zyada se zyada liquid den
 Allow them to drink home-made juice, lemon water or coconut water
 bachche ko chacha, taaje falon kaa ras, milk shaike bhi de sakate hai

 inke seven se bachche ke sharir main pani kii kami nahin hogi
 - During the summer days, make children habit of bathing twice a day
 bachche ko sooti kapade hi pahanaaen or kapadon ko rojaanaa badalen
 If you come from outside, get his hands and feet thoroughly cleaned with soap
 aisa karne se sankraman kaa khatra kam ho jayega
 Take care of the cold and warm weather, eg, if the children come back after playing in the sun, do not let them sit in front of the cooler and do not give cold water immediately
 - garmi ke mausam menconjuctivitis hone kaa khatra bhi bad jaataa he

 isse bacchon kii ankhon main dryness bhi nahin hogi
 - Children often have heat and sunburn problems in summer

 sahitya kii duniya main vijay tendulkar kii kalam bade-bade kalamkaaron kii bolti band kar detii he

 jaanate hai unke baaren main- vijay kaa janm 6 janvari 1928 ko maharashtra ke kolhapur main ek brahman parivaar main hua

 ghazal ko har jubaan tak pahunchane vaale dushyant kumaar ko salaam- vijay hi aise lekhak the jinhone marathi theatre ko ek nai oonchaaiyaan deen
 Tendulkar, who has been active for more than five decades, wrote stories and novels besides writing for theater and films
 - unke naatak aksar kalpana se pare hote the
 He loved writing out of the box
 vahiin apane li se hatakar kahaniyaan likhane ke kaaran unhen naatakon kaa virodh bhi jhelana padaa

 saat suron ke sabase bade fankaar mohammad rafee kaa aaj janmdin he

 donon senior tiimon ke bich bhale hi world cap main pehali baar koi semifinal muqabla khelaa ja rahaa ho, lekin 2008 ke junior world cap ke semifinal main in donon captainon kii aguwai main timen pehle bhi utar chuki hai
 After 11 years, 10 such coincidences will surprise you in the initial phase of the match again
 2008 kaa wo semifinal or aaj ke semifinal mukaable main kai rochak samanthaayen hai jo har kisi ko chaunkaa denge
 Apart from being the same captain of both teams, there are 10 more interesting similarities
 1
 New Zealand won the toss in both semifinal matches and on both occasions the Kiwi team decided to bat first
 2
 The New Zealand team, who decided to bat first, suffered the first blow in the fourth over
 2019 ke world cap main pari ke chauthe over kii teesri gend par bharat ne pehla wicket jhatka
 Whereas in the 2008 World Cup, the wicket fell on the first ball of the fourth over
 3
 New Zealand's first wicket fell as the first opener
 2008 main match kii pehla gend khilne vaale jorge varkar out hue to 2019 ke match main pehali ball khilne vaale martin gaptil out hue
 4
 bharat ko pehla wicket kaich out ke rup main mila
 New Zealand's first batsman was caught out in the 2008 and 2019 matches
 2008 main saurav tiwari ne to 2019 main viraat kohli ne kaich lapka
 5
 newjiland kii ore se out hone vaale pehle ballebaaj donon hi maichon main dahaai ke aankade ko nahin chhu sake
 George Worker was dismissed for just 3 runs in 2008 and Martin Guptill 1 run in the 2019 World Cup
 6
 In both semifinal matches, the first success was given to India by the second number bowler
 2019 main bhubaneshwar kumaar ke saath gendbaaji shuru karne vaale jasprit bumraah ne team ke liye pehla wicket jhatka, to vahiin 2008 main pradeep sangwan ke saath gendbaaji shuru karne vaale ajitesh argal ne bharat ke liye pehla wicket jhatka
 7
 2008 or 2019 ke world cap main bharat ke liye gendbaaji kii shuruyaat karne vaale donon hi gendbaajon ne shuruaati spel main ek madan over bhi daalaa
 In 2008, Pradeep Sangwan and in 2019, Bhuvneshwar Kumar bowled a maiden over
 8
 There are 4 such players playing in the semi-finals, who were also in the 2008 Under-19 World Cup

 9
 viraat kohli 2008 ke under-19 world cap main team india ke captain the to newjiland kii ore se ken williamsan ne team kii aguwai kii, 11 saal baad phir se donon hi apni-apni team kii aguwai kar rahe hai

 10
 viraat kohli ke alaava ravindra jadeja bhi 2008 or 2019 world cap kii team kaa hissaa rahe
